This format is deprecated, and in the future the new format will always be used."}},"query":{"normalized":[{"from":"Cody_Canada","to":"Cody Canada"}],"pages":{"17026099":{"pageid":17026099,"ns":0,"title":"Cody Canada","revisions":[{"contentformat":"text/x-wiki","contentmodel":"wikitext","*":"{{short description|American rock/alt-country musician|bot=PearBOT 5}}\n{{Use mdy dates|date=September 2020}}\n{{Infobox musical artist\n| name            = Cody Canada\n| image           = CodyCanadaApr09.jpg\n| alt             =\n| caption         = Cody Canada performing in April 2009\n| image_size      =\n| birth_date      = {{birth date and age|1976|5|25}}\n| origin          = [[Pampa, Texas]]\n| instrument      = Guitar, [[mandolin]], harmonica\n| genre           = Rock, [[Alternative Country]], [[Country Rock]], [[Red Dirt (music)|Red Dirt]]\n| occupation      = Singer-songwriter\n| years_active    = 1994\u2013present\n| label           = Underground Sound\n| associated_acts = [[Cross Canadian Ragweed]], [[The Departed (band)|The Departed]], [[Mike McClure]], [[Jason Boland & the Stragglers]], [[Stoney LaRue]], [[Dierks Bentley]], [[Randy Rogers]], [[Reckless Kelly]], [[Robert Earl Keen]], [[James McMurtry]], [[ZZ Top]], [[Shooter Jennings]], Seth James, [[Ray Wylie Hubbard]], [[Medicine Show]], [[Todd Snider]], [[craig Gerdes]], [[Wade Bowen]]\n| website         = {{URL|www.thedepartedmusic.com}}\n}}\n\n'''Cody Jay Canada''' (born May 25, 1976) is an American rock/[[alt-country]] musician who currently is the lead singer and lead guitarist of the rock band [[The Departed (band)|The Departed]] since 2010. From 1994 to 2010, Canada was the lead singer of rock/alt country band [[Cross Canadian Ragweed]].<ref name=\"allmusic\">{{cite web|url={{AllMusic|class=artist|id=mn0000087099|pure_url=yes}}|title=Cody Canada Biography|last=Deming|first=Mark|work=[[Allmusic]]|accessdate=July 31, 2012}}</ref>\n\n==Early life==\nCanada was born in [[Pampa, Texas]], in 1976. He acquired a taste for music after attending a [[George Strait]] concert with his parents at the age of four. The next day he asked for a guitar.  Canada first started playing guitar at the age of eight. While Cody was a teen, the Canada family relocated to [[Yukon, Oklahoma]]. As a teenager Canada was drawn to rock bands such as [[Nirvana (band)|Nirvana]] and [[Pearl Jam]] and also [[outlaw country]].<ref name=\"allmusic\" />\n\n==Cross Canadian Ragweed==\n{{main|Cross Canadian Ragweed}}\nIn 1994, Canada along with fellow musicians Matt Weidemann (bass), Grady Cross (guitar), and Randy Ragsdale (percussion) formed Cross Canadian Ragweed in [[Yukon, Oklahoma]]. The band was named after the original members with Canada taking on the role of lead guitarist, lead vocals, and prominent songwriter. They would later move to [[Stillwater, Oklahoma]]. From the time of Ragweed's formation until its end in 2010, the band released seven studio albums as well as three live albums.\n\nIn 2010, the band went on an extended hiatus due to slight tensions inside the band, and Ragsdale's family responsibilities, eventually breaking up in late 2010.\n\n==The Departed==\n{{main|The Departed (band)}}\nIn 2011, Canada and Plato formed a new band, initially called Cody Canada & the Departed. The band originally consisted of Canada (guitar/vocals), Plato (bass guitar/vocals), Seth James (guitar/vocals), Steve Littleton (keyboards) and Chris Doege (drums) who replaced original drummer, Dave Bowen. They released their first album in June 2011 titled ''This Is Indian Land'', consisting of covers written by Oklahoma songwriters.\n\nOn August 24, 2012, the band, now billing themselves as The Departed, announced through their website and social media that they would release their first original album titled ''Adventus''. The album was released on November 13, 2012.\n\nIn September 2012, the band announced that they would release one song from ''Adventus'' every Monday leading up until the album's release on their Facebook artist profile.\n\nIn 2014 the band announced a third studio album.  ''Hippielovepunk'' was released on January 13, 2015.  The album debut at No. 9 on the Billboard US Country chart as well as No. 9 on the US Indie chart.  The first single was a return to the Red Dirt sound of CCR titled ''Inbetweener''.\n\n==Solo work and collaborations==\nOn November 19, 2013, Cody Canada released a solo acoustic 2-disc album ''[[Some Old, Some New, Maybe a Cover or Two]]''.  The album was recorded live at Third Coast Music in [[Port Aransas, Texas]], with 19 songs from throughout Canada's career, including works with Cross Canadian Ragweed and The Departed.<ref>{{cite web |url= http://radiotexaslive.com/the-new-album-from-cody-canada-some-old-some-new-maybe-a-cover-or-two-out-today/ |title=The New Album from Cody Canada 'Some Old, Some New, Maybe A Cover Or Two,' Out Today|author=Buddy Logan |date=November 19, 2013 |work=Radio Texas Live}}</ref>\n\nOn November 13, 2015, Cody Canada released a two-disc, 35-track album with [[Mike McClure]], ''Chip and Ray, Together Again for the First Time''.  The album was recorded in Port Aransas, Texas, and features songs they worked on or recorded together.<ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.wideopencountry.com/cody-canada-mike-mcclure-team-new-album-chip-ray/|title=Cody Canada and Mike McClure Team up for New Album, 'Chip & Ray'|author=Edward Mack|work=Wide Open Country|access-date=December 4, 2015|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20160304035456/http://www.wideopencountry.com/cody-canada-mike-mcclure-team-new-album-chip-ray/|archive-date=March 4, 2016|url-status=dead}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |url=http://roughstock.com/news/2015/11/39384-top-10-country-albums-chart-november-23-2015 |title=Top 10 Country Albums Chart: November 23, 2015|first= Matt |last=Bjorke |date= November 21, 2015 }}</ref>\n\n==Personal life==\nCanada is married to Shannon O\u2019Neal Canada, who also manages The Departed and their label Underground Sound. He has two sons, Dierks Cobain Canada (named after personal friend and country singer [[Dierks Bentley]] and former Nirvana lead singer [[Kurt Cobain]]), and Willy Vedder Canada (named after [[Reckless Kelly (band)|Reckless Kelly]] member Willy Braun and [[Pearl Jam]]'s long time lead singer [[Eddie Vedder]]). Dierks plays in a band called Waves, and has been featured in live shows with Cody.<ref>{{Cite web|last1=Editor|first1=Terence J. Fitzwater|last2=Publisher|title=Family that plays together stays together|url=https://gonzalesinquirer.com/stories/family-that-plays-together-stays-together,27084|access-date=2021-01-20|website=The Gonzales Inquirer|date=December 5, 2019 |language=en}}</ref> He is also the brother in law of fellow red dirt musician [[Wade Bowen]], who married his sister-in-law Shelby. Canada is also a [[Christians|Christian]], and has mentioned his faith and [[Jesus Christ]] in Ragweed songs \"The President Song\" (''Live and Loud at the Wormy Dog Saloon'', 2001) , \"Highway 377\" (''Highway 377'', 2001), \"Carry You Home\" (''Cross Canadian Ragweed'', 2002), \"Down\" (''Soul Gravy'', 2004), and \"When it All Goes Down\" (''Garage'', 2005). Canada lives with his family in [[New Braunfels, Texas]].\n\n==Awards and achievements==\n2023 Trailblazer Award, Texas Country Music Association\n\n==Discography==\n\n===Studio albums===\n{| class=\"wikitable plainrowheaders\" style=\"text-align:center;\"\n|-\n!
